type=3D"always">
    <t:objective>Create test accounts</t:objective>
  =20
    <!-- Login to admin -->
    <t:test>
        <t:request>
            <AuthRequest xmlns=3D"urn:zimbraAdmin">

                <password>${admin.password}</password>

        </t:request>

    </t:test>

<t:test_case testcaseid=3D"outlook_ical_basic01" type=3D"functional">
    <t:objective>Verify the basic iCal format invitation with basic =
information </t:objective>
    <t:steps>
              1. Use lmtp inject to inject the message
              2. Login as the invitee
              3. GetApptSummaries, verify the basic information : =
subject,location,notes and attachment
    </t:steps>
   =20
    <t:test>
        <t:lmtpInjectRequest>
            <filename>${appt1.file}</filename>
            <to>${account3.name}</to>
            <from>${account2.name}</from>
            <server>${defaultdomain.name}</server>
        </t:lmtpInjectRequest>
    </t:test>

    <t:test delay=3D"${postfixdelay.msec}">
        <t:request>
            <AuthRequest xmlns=3D"urn:zimbraAccount">
                <account by=3D"name">${account3.name}</account>
                <password>${defaultpassword.value}</password>
            </AuthRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path=3D"//acct:AuthResponse/acct:authToken" =
set=3D"authToken"/>
            <t:select path=3D"//acct:AuthResponse/acct:sessionId" =
set=3D"sessionId"/>=20
        </t:response>
    </t:test>
   =20
    <!-- do a simple verification of the mail -->
    <t:test>
        <t:request>
            <SearchRequest xmlns=3D"urn:zimbraMail" =
types=3D"message,appointment">
                  <query>subject:${mail1.subject}</query>
            </SearchRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m" attr=3D"su" =
match=3D"${mail1.subject}"/>
            <t:select =
path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m/mail:inv/mail:comp" attr=3D"loc" =
match=3D"${appt.location}"/>
            <t:select =
path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m/mail:inv/mail:comp" attr=3D"name" =
match=3D"${appt1.summary}"/>
            <t:select =
path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m/mail:inv/mail:comp/mail:s" =
attr=3D"d" match=3D"${appt1.start}"/>
            <t:select =
path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m/mail:inv/mail:comp/mail:e" =
attr=3D"d" match=3D"${appt1.end}"/>
            <t:select =
path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m/mail:inv/mail:comp/mail:at" =
attr=3D"url" match=3D"${appt.invitee2}"/>
            <t:select path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m/mail:e" =
attr=3D"a" match=3D"${appt.organizer}"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

</t:test_case>

        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m" attr=3D"su" =

            <t:select =

            <t:select =

            <t:select =

            <t:select path=3D"//mail:SearchResponse/mail:m/mail:e" =

        </t:response>
    </t:test>
